<h5 id="codeguiimportfilecode"><a href="#codeguiimportfilecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>guiImportFile</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Invokes the <em>Import... (Ctrl+Shift+I)</em> dialog with an optional file path. Brings up the dialog for user to review the import. Supports all file types that Anki supports. Brings open file dialog if no path is provided. Forward slashes must be used in the path on Windows. Only supported for Anki 2.1.52+.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"guiImportFile"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"path"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"C:/Users/Desktop/cards.txt"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeguiexitankicode"><a href="#codeguiexitankicode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>guiExitAnki</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Schedules a request to gracefully close Anki. This operation is asynchronous, so it will return immediately and
won't wait until the Anki process actually terminates.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"guiExitAnki"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeguicheckdatabasecode"><a href="#codeguicheckdatabasecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>guiCheckDatabase</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Requests a database check, but returns immediately without waiting for the check to complete. Therefore, the action will always return <code>true</code> even if errors are detected during the database check.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"guiCheckDatabase"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<hr/>
<h4 id="media-actions"><a href="#media-actions" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a>Media Actions</h4>
<h5 id="codestoremediafilecode"><a href="#codestoremediafilecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>storeMediaFile</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Stores a file with the specified base64-encoded contents inside the media folder. Alternatively you can specify a
absolute file path, or a url from where the file shell be downloaded. If more than one of <code>data</code>, <code>path</code> and <code>url</code> are provided, the <code>data</code> field will be used first, then <code>path</code>, and finally <code>url</code>. To prevent Anki from removing files not used by any cards (e.g. for configuration files), prefix the filename with an underscore. These files are still synchronized to AnkiWeb.
Any existing file with the same name is deleted by default. Set <code>deleteExisting</code> to false to prevent that
by <a href="https://github.com/ankitects/anki/blob/aeba725d3ea9628c73300648f748140db3fdd5ed/rslib/src/media/files.rs#L194" rel="nofollow noopener">letting Anki give the new file a non-conflicting name</a>.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request (relative path):</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"storeMediaFile"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"filename"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"_hello.txt"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"data"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"SGVsbG8sIHdvcmxkIQ=="</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
<p><em>Content of <code>_hello.txt</code></em>:</p>
<pre><code>Hello world!
</code></pre>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result (relative path):</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"_hello.txt"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>

<h4 id="miscellaneous-actions"><a href="#miscellaneous-actions" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a>Miscellaneous Actions</h4>
<h5 id="coderequestpermissioncode"><a href="#coderequestpermissioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>requestPermission</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Requests permission to use the API exposed by this plugin. This method does not require the API key, and is the
only one that accepts requests from any origin; the other methods only accept requests from trusted origins,
which are listed under <code>webCorsOriginList</code> in the add-on config. <code>localhost</code> is trusted by default.</p>
<p>Calling this method from an untrusted origin will display a popup in Anki asking the user whether they want to
allow your origin to use the API; calls from trusted origins will return the result without displaying the popup.
When denying permission, the user may also choose to ignore further permission requests from that origin. These
origins end up in the <code>ignoreOriginList</code>, editable via the add-on config.</p>
<p>The result always contains the <code>permission</code> field, which in turn contains either the string <code>granted</code> or <code>denied</code>,
corresponding to whether your origin is trusted. If your origin is trusted, the fields <code>requireApiKey</code> (<code>true</code> if
required) and <code>version</code> will also be returned.</p>
<p>This should be the first call you make to make sure that your application and Anki-Connect are able to communicate
properly with each other. New versions of Anki-Connect are backwards compatible; as long as you are using actions
which are available in the reported Anki-Connect version or earlier, everything should work fine.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"requestPermission"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample results:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"permission"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"granted"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"requireApiKey"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"permission"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"denied"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeversioncode"><a href="#codeversioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>version</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Gets the version of the API exposed by this plugin. Currently versions <code>1</code> through <code>6</code> are defined.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"version"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeapireflectcode"><a href="#codeapireflectcode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>apiReflect</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Gets information about the AnkiConnect APIs available. The request supports the following params:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>scopes</code> - An array of scopes to get reflection information about.
The only currently supported value is <code>"actions"</code>.</li>
<li><code>actions</code> - Either <code>null</code> or an array of API method names to check for.
If the value is <code>null</code>, the result will list all of the available API actions.
If the value is an array of strings, the result will only contain actions which were in this array.</li>
</ul>
<p>The result will contain a list of which scopes were used and a value for each scope.
For example, the <code>"actions"</code> scope will contain a <code>"actions"</code> property which contains a list of supported action names.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"apiReflect"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"scopes"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"actions"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"invalidType"</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"actions"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"apiReflect"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"invalidMethod"</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"scopes"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"actions"</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"actions"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"apiReflect"</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>

<h5 id="codeloadprofilecode"><a href="#codeloadprofilecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>loadProfile</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Selects the profile specified in request.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"loadProfile"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"user1"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codemulticode"><a href="#codemulticode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>multi</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Performs multiple actions in one request, returning an array with the response of each action (in the given order).</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"multi"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"actions"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"deckNames"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"deckNames"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"invalidAction"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"useless"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"param"</span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"invalidAction"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"useless"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"param"</span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"unsupported action"</span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"unsupported action"</span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeexportpackagecode"><a href="#codeexportpackagecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>exportPackage</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Exports a given deck in <code>.apkg</code> format. Returns <code>true</code> if successful or <code>false</code> otherwise. The optional property
<code>includeSched</code> (default is <code>false</code>) can be specified to include the cards' scheduling data.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"exportPackage"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"deck"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"path"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"/data/Deck.apkg"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"includeSched"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeimportpackagecode"><a href="#codeimportpackagecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>importPackage</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Imports a file in <code>.apkg</code> format into the collection. Returns <code>true</code> if successful or <code>false</code> otherwise.
Note that the file path is relative to Anki's collection.media folder, not to the client.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"importPackage"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"path"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"/data/Deck.apkg"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codereloadcollectioncode"><a href="#codereloadcollectioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>reloadCollection</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Tells anki to reload all data from the database.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"reloadCollection"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<details>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

</details>
<details>

<h5 id="codefindmodelsbynamecode"><a href="#codefindmodelsbynamecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>findModelsByName</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Gets a list of models for the provided model names from the current user.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"findModelsByName"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelNames"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic (and reversed card)"</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>

<h5 id="codemodelfieldnamescode"><a href="#codemodelfieldnamescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelFieldNames</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Gets the complete list of field names for the provided model name.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"modelFieldNames"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Front"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Back"</span><span class="p">],</span>

<span class="p">}</span>

</details>

<h5 id="codemodelfieldsontemplatescode"><a href="#codemodelfieldsontemplatescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelFieldsOnTemplates</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Returns an object indicating the fields on the question and answer side of each card template for the given model
name. The question side is given first in each array.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"modelFieldsOnTemplates"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic (and reversed card)"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"Card 1"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[[</span><span class="s2">"Front"</span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Back"</span><span class="p">]],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"Card 2"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[[</span><span class="s2">"Back"</span><span class="p">],</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"Front"</span><span class="p">]]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codecreatemodelcode"><a href="#codecreatemodelcode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>createModel</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Creates a new model to be used in Anki. User must provide the <code>modelName</code>, <code>inOrderFields</code> and <code>cardTemplates</code> to be
used in the model. There are optional fields <code>css</code> and <code>isCloze</code>. If not specified, <code>css</code> will use the default Anki css and <code>isCloze</code> will be equal to <code>false</code>. If <code>isCloze</code> is <code>true</code> then model will be created as Cloze.</p>
<p>Optionally the <code>Name</code> field can be provided for each entry of <code>cardTemplates</code>. By default the
card names will be <code>Card 1</code>, <code>Card 2</code>, and so on.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>

<h5 id="codemodeltemplatescode"><a href="#codemodeltemplatescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelTemplates</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Returns an object indicating the template content for each card connected to the provided model by name.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"modelTemplates"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic (and reversed card)"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"Card 1"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{Front}}"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{FrontSide}}\n\n&lt;hr id=answer&gt;\n\n{{Back}}"</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"Card 2"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{Back}}"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{FrontSide}}\n\n&lt;hr id=answer&gt;\n\n{{Front}}"</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<h5 id="codeupdatemodeltemplatescode"><a href="#codeupdatemodeltemplatescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>updateModelTemplates</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Modify the templates of an existing model by name. Only specifies cards and specified sides will be modified.
If an existing card or side is not included in the request, it will be left unchanged.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"updateModelTemplates"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"model"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Custom"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"templates"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Card 1"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{Question}}?"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"{{Answer}}!"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>

<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"name"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Custom"</span><span class="p">,</span>

<h5 id="codefindandreplaceinmodelscode"><a href="#codefindandreplaceinmodelscode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>findAndReplaceInModels</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Find and replace string in existing model by model name. Customise to replace in front, back or css by setting to true/false.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"findAndReplaceInModels"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"model"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">""</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"findText"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"text_to_replace"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"replaceText"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"replace_with_text"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"css"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<h5 id="codemodeltemplaterenamecode"><a href="#codemodeltemplaterenamecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelTemplateRename</code></h5>

<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"oldTemplateName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Card 1"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"newTemplateName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Card 1 renamed"</span>

<h5 id="codemodeltemplaterepositioncode"><a href="#codemodeltemplaterepositioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelTemplateReposition</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Repositions a template in an existing model.</p>
<p>The value of <code>index</code> starts at 0. For example, an index of <code>0</code> puts the template in the first position, and an index of <code>2</code> puts the template in the third position.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"modelTemplateReposition"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"templateName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Card 1"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"index"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

</details>

<h5 id="codemodelfieldrepositioncode"><a href="#codemodelfieldrepositioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelFieldReposition</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Reposition the field within the field list of a given model.</p>
<p>The value of <code>index</code> starts at 0. For example, an index of <code>0</code> puts the field in the first position, and an index of <code>2</code> puts the field in the third position.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"modelFieldReposition"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"fieldName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Back"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"index"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>

<h5 id="codemodelfieldaddcode"><a href="#codemodelfieldaddcode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelFieldAdd</code></h5>

<h5 id="codemodelfieldsetdescriptioncode"><a href="#codemodelfieldsetdescriptioncode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>modelFieldSetDescription</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Sets the description (the text seen in the gui editor when a field is empty) for a field within a given model.</p>
<p>Older versions of Anki (2.1.49 and below) do not have field descriptions. In that case, this will return with <code>false</code>.</p>
<details>

<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>

<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"fieldName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Front"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"description"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"example field description"</span>

<hr/>
<h4 id="note-actions"><a href="#note-actions" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a>Note Actions</h4>
<h5 id="codeaddnotecode"><a href="#codeaddnotecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>addNote</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Creates a note using the given deck and model, with the provided field values and tags. Returns the identifier of
the created note created on success, and <code>null</code> on failure.</p>
<p>Anki-Connect can download audio, video, and picture files and embed them in newly created notes. The corresponding <code>audio</code>, <code>video</code>, and <code>picture</code> note members are
optional and can be omitted. If you choose to include any of them, they should contain a single object or an array of objects
with the mandatory <code>filename</code> field and one of <code>data</code>, <code>path</code> or <code>url</code>. Refer to the documentation of <code>storeMediaFile</code> for an explanation of these fields.
The <code>skipHash</code> field can be optionally provided to skip the inclusion of files with an MD5 hash that matches the provided value.
This is useful for avoiding the saving of error pages and stub files.
The <code>fields</code> member is a list of fields that should play audio or video, or show a picture when the card is displayed in
Anki. The <code>allowDuplicate</code> member inside <code>options</code> group can be set to true to enable adding duplicate cards.
Normally duplicate cards can not be added and trigger exception.</p>
<p>The <code>duplicateScope</code> member inside <code>options</code> can be used to specify the scope for which duplicates are checked.
A value of <code>"deck"</code> will only check for duplicates in the target deck; any other value will check the entire collection.</p>
<p>The <code>duplicateScopeOptions</code> object can be used to specify some additional settings:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>duplicateScopeOptions.deckName</code> will specify which deck to use for checking duplicates in. If undefined or <code>null</code>, the target deck will be used.</li>
<li><code>duplicateScopeOptions.checkChildren</code> will change whether or not duplicate cards are checked in child decks. The default value is <code>false</code>.</li>
<li><code>duplicateScopeOptions.checkAllModels</code> specifies whether duplicate checks are performed across all note types. The default value is <code>false</code>.</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"addNote"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"note"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"front content"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"back content"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"options"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"allowDuplicate"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"duplicateScope"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"deck"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"duplicateScopeOptions"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"checkChildren"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"checkAllModels"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="s2">"yomichan"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"audio"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[{</span>

<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"filename"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"yomichan_ねこ_猫.mp3"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"skipHash"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"7e2c2f954ef6051373ba916f000168dc"</span><span class="p">,</span>

<h5 id="codeaddnotescode"><a href="#codeaddnotescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>addNotes</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Creates multiple notes using the given deck and model, with the provided field values and tags. Returns an array of
identifiers of the created notes. In the event of any errors, all errors are gathered and returned.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Please see the documentation for <code>addNote</code> for an explanation of objects in the <code>notes</code> array.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"addNotes"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:{</span>
<span class="w">      </span><span class="nt">"notes"</span><span class="p">:[</span>
<span class="w">         </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"College::PluginDev"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"non_existent_model"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:{</span>
<span class="w">               </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"front"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">               </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"bak"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">         </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">         </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"College::PluginDev"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:{</span>
<span class="w">               </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"front"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">               </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"bak"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">         </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">      </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">   </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"['model was not found: non_existent_model']"</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codecanaddnotescode"><a href="#codecanaddnotescode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>canAddNotes</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Accepts an array of objects which define parameters for candidate notes (see <code>addNote</code>) and returns an array of
booleans indicating whether or not the parameters at the corresponding index could be used to create a new note.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"canAddNotes"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"notes"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"front content"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"back content"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="s2">"yomichan"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="kc">true</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codecanaddnoteswitherrordetailcode"><a href="#codecanaddnoteswitherrordetailcode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>canAddNotesWithErrorDetail</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Accepts an array of objects which define parameters for candidate notes (see <code>addNote</code>) and returns an array of
objects with fields <code>canAdd</code> and <code>error</code>.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>canAdd</code> indicates whether or not the parameters at the corresponding index could be used to create a new note.</li>
<li><code>error</code> contains an explanation of why a note cannot be added.</li>
</ul>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"canAddNotesWithErrorDetail"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"notes"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"front content"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"back content"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="s2">"yomichan"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"deckName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"front content 2"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"back content 2"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="s2">"yomichan"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"canAdd"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"cannot create note because it is a duplicate"</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"canAdd"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">true</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeupdatenotefieldscode"><a href="#codeupdatenotefieldscode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>updateNoteFields</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Modify the fields of an existing note. You can also include audio, video, or picture files which will be added to the note with an
optional <code>audio</code>, <code>video</code>, or <code>picture</code> property. Please see the documentation for <code>addNote</code> for an explanation of objects in the <code>audio</code>, <code>video</code>, or <code>picture</code> array.</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Warning</strong>:
You must not be viewing the note that you are updating on your Anki browser, otherwise
the fields will not update. See <a href="https://github.com/FooSoft/anki-connect/issues/82" rel="nofollow noopener">this issue</a>
for further details.</p>
</blockquote>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"updateNoteFields"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"note"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1514547547030</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new front content"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new back content"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"audio"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"url"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"https://assets.languagepod101.com/dictionary/japanese/audiomp3.php?kanji=猫&amp;kana=ねこ"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"filename"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"yomichan_ねこ_猫.mp3"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"skipHash"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"7e2c2f954ef6051373ba916f000168dc"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">                    </span><span class="s2">"Front"</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">}]</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeupdatenotecode"><a href="#codeupdatenotecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>updateNote</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Modify the fields and/or tags of an existing note.
In other words, combines <code>updateNoteFields</code> and <code>updateNoteTags</code>.
Please see their documentation for an explanation of all properties.</p>
<p>Either <code>fields</code> or <code>tags</code> property can be omitted without affecting the other.
Thus valid requests to <code>updateNoteFields</code> also work with <code>updateNote</code>.
The note must have the <code>fields</code> property in order to update the optional audio, video, or picture objects.</p>
<p>If neither <code>fields</code> nor <code>tags</code> are provided, the method will fail.
Fields are updated first and are not rolled back if updating tags fails.
Tags are not updated if updating fields fails.</p>
<blockquote>
<p><strong>Warning</strong>
You must not be viewing the note that you are updating on your Anki browser, otherwise
the fields will not update. See <a href="https://github.com/FooSoft/anki-connect/issues/82" rel="nofollow noopener">this issue</a>
for further details.</p>
</blockquote>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"updateNote"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"note"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1514547547030</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new front content"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new back content"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"new"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"tags"</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codeupdatenotemodelcode"><a href="#codeupdatenotemodelcode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>updateNoteModel</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Update the model, fields, and tags of an existing note.
This allows you to change the note's model, update its fields with new content, and set new tags.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"updateNoteModel"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"note"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1514547547030</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"NewModel"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"NewField1"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new field 1"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"NewField2"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new field 2"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"NewField3"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"new field 3"</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="s2">"new"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"updated"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"tags"</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>

<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"query"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"deck:current"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>

<h5 id="codenotesinfocode"><a href="#codenotesinfocode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>notesInfo</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Returns a list of objects containing for each note ID the note fields, tags, note type, modification time,the cards belonging to
the note and the profile where the note was created.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request (note ids):</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"notesInfo"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"notes"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1502298033753</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request (query):</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"notesInfo"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"query"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"deck:current"</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"noteId"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="mi">1502298033753</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"profile"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"User_1"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"modelName"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"Basic"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"tags"</span><span class="p">:[</span><span class="s2">"tag"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="s2">"another_tag"</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"fields"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Front"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"value"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"front content"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"order"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"Back"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span><span class="nt">"value"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"back content"</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="nt">"order"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"mod"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1718377864</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="nt">"cards"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1498938915662</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
s
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codenotesmodtimecode"><a href="#codenotesmodtimecode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>notesModTime</code></h5>

<h5 id="codegetnumcardsreviewedtodaycode"><a href="#codegetnumcardsreviewedtodaycode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>getNumCardsReviewedToday</code></h5>
