<h5 id="codecardreviewscode"><a href="#codecardreviewscode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>cardReviews</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Requests all card reviews for a specified deck after a certain time.
<code>startID</code> is the latest unix time not included in the result.
Returns a list of 9-tuples <code>(reviewTime, cardID, usn, buttonPressed, newInterval, previousInterval, newFactor, reviewDuration, reviewType)</code></p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"cardReviews"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"deck"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"default"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"startID"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1594194095740</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1594194095746</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1485369733217</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">   </span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2500</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6157</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1594201393292</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1485369902086</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">    </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">4846</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
<h5 id="codegetreviewsofcardscode"><a href="#codegetreviewsofcardscode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>getReviewsOfCards</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Requests all card reviews for each card ID.
Returns a dictionary mapping each card ID to a list of dictionaries of the format:</p>
<pre><code>{
    "id": reviewTime,
    "usn": usn,
    "ease": buttonPressed,
    "ivl": newInterval,
    "lastIvl": previousInterval,
    "factor": newFactor,
    "time": reviewDuration,
    "type": reviewType,
}
</code></pre>
<p>The reason why these key values are used instead of the more descriptive counterparts
is because these are the exact key values used in Anki's database.</p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"getReviewsOfCards"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"cards"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="s2">"1653613948202"</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"1653613948202"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1653772912146</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"usn"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1750</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"ease"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"ivl"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-20</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"lastIvl"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-20</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"factor"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"time"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">38192</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">},</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"id"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1653772965429</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"usn"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1750</span><span class="p">,</span>

<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"factor"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"time"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">15337</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">                </span><span class="nt">"type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span>

<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"deck"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"default"</span>

<h5 id="codeinsertreviewscode"><a href="#codeinsertreviewscode" rel="nofollow noopener">#</a><code>insertReviews</code></h5>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Inserts the given reviews into the database. Required format: list of 9-tuples <code>(reviewTime, cardID, usn, buttonPressed, newInterval, previousInterval, newFactor, reviewDuration, reviewType)</code></p>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample request:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"action"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="s2">"insertReviews"</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"version"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"params"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="nt">"reviews"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="p">[</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1594194095746</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1485369733217</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">3</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">   </span><span class="mi">4</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">2500</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">6157</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">],</span>
<span class="w">            </span><span class="p">[</span><span class="mi">1594201393292</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1485369902086</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">1</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">-60</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w">    </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">4846</span><span class="p">,</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="mi">0</span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">        </span><span class="p">]</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="p">}</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><i>Sample result:</i></summary>
<div class="highlight"><pre><span></span><span class="p">{</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"result"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span><span class="p">,</span>
<span class="w">    </span><span class="nt">"error"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="w"> </span><span class="kc">null</span>
<span class="p">}</span>
</pre></div>
</details>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
